			flag = LONG_MARCH_LOC_Hubei
			flag = LONG_MARCH_DEF_Hubei
			not = { flag = LONG_MARCH_SIDE }
			flag = { which = LONG_MARCH_FATIGUE when = 0 value = 3 }  #Fatigue equal exactly to 3
		}
		#ai_chance = 10
		name = EVT_1330110067_ACTION4
		#reduces strength of communist forces by 40 000
		command = { type = setflag which = LONG_MARCH_CHC when = 1 value = -40 }
		command = { trigger = { and = { flag = { which = LONG_MARCH_CHC when = 2 value = 0 }  not = { flag = LONG_MARCH_LOC_Shaanxi } } } type = event where = CHC when = 15 which = 1330110064 }
		command = { trigger = { NOT= { flag = LONG_MARCH_CHC } } type = event where = CHC when = 0 which = 1330110068 }
		command = { trigger = { flag = LONG_MARCH_LOC_Shaanxi flag = { which = LONG_MARCH_CHC when = 2 value = 0 } } type = event where = CHC when = 0 which = 1330110069 }
	}
